) AS [t2] ON [c].[Id] = [t2].[BannerImageId]

    SELECT [c1].[Id], [c1].[BannerButtonText], [c1].[BannerText], [c1].[ButtonLink], [c1].[ButtonText], [c1].[ContentData], [c1].[ContentOrderNo], [c1].[ContentPageId], [c1].[ContentShort], [c1].[ContentTypesId], [c1].[CreaDate], [c1].[CreaUser], [c1].[Description], [c1].[ExternalLink], [c1].[FormTypeId], [c1].[IsActive], [c1].[IsBayi], [c1].[IsBireysel], [c1].[IsClick], [c1].[IsDeleted], [c1].[IsEndustri], [c1].[IsFooterMenu], [c1].[IsGallery], [c1].[IsHamburgerMenu], [c1].[IsHeaderMenu], [c1].[IsInteral], [c1].[IsInterax], [c1].[IsIntersecure], [c1].[IsInterwall], [c1].[IsMap], [c1].[IsMimar], [c1].[IsPublish], [c1].[IsSideMenu], [c1].[IsStatus], [c1].[LangId], [c1].[Link], [c1].[LoginCount], [c1].[MetaDescription], [c1].[MetaKeywords], [c1].[MetaTitle], [c1].[ModDate], [c1].[ModUser], [c1].[Name], [c1].[OrderNo], [c1].[OrjId], [c1].[OrjId1], [c1].[TemplateType], [c1].[VideoLink]
    FROM [ContentPage] AS [c1]
    WHERE [c1].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t3] ON [c].[Id] = [t3].[ContentPageId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d2].[Id], [d2].[Alt], [d2].[BIMFileId], [d2].[BannerImageId], [d2].[CadDataId], [d2].[CreaDate], [d2].[CreaUser], [d2].[DocumentId], [d2].[GalleryId], [d2].[Guid], [d2].[IsDeleted], [d2].[IsStatus], [d2].[Link], [d2].[LoginCount], [d2].[ModDate], [d2].[ModUser], [d2].[Name], [d2].[OrderNo], [d2].[PictureId], [d2].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d2].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d2].[ThumbImageId], [d2].[Title], [d2].[Types], [d2].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d2]
    WHERE [d2].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t4] ON [c].[Id] = [t4].[GalleryId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [d3].[Id], [d3].[Alt], [d3].[BIMFileId], [d3].[BannerImageId], [d3].[CadDataId], [d3].[CreaDate], [d3].[CreaUser], [d3].[DocumentId], [d3].[GalleryId], [d3].[Guid], [d3].[IsDeleted], [d3].[IsStatus], [d3].[Link], [d3].[LoginCount], [d3].[ModDate], [d3].[ModUser], [d3].[Name], [d3].[OrderNo], [d3].[PictureId], [d3].[TechnicalDocumentId], [d3].[TechnicalPropertyId], [d3].[ThumbImageId], [d3].[Title], [d3].[Types], [d3].[data_class]
    FROM [Documents] AS [d3]
    WHERE [d3].[IsDeleted] IS NULL
) AS [t5] ON [c].[Id] = [t5].[DocumentId]
WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] IS NULL AND (((([c].[LangId] = @__langID_0) AND [c].[IsDeleted] IS NULL) AND ([c].[IsPublish] = CAST(1 AS bit))) AND ([c].[IsInteral] = CAST(1 AS bit)))
ORDER BY [c].[Id], [t].[Id], [t0].[Id], [t1].[Id], [t2].[Id], [t3].[Id], [t4].[Id], [t5].[Id]"
